Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

017551,000026:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017552,000027:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017553,000028:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017554,000029:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017555,000030: 
017556,000031:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017557,000032: 
017558,000033:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017559,000034:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017560,000035:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017561,000036:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017562,000037:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017563,000038:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017564,000039:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017565,000040:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017566,000041:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017567,000042: 
017568,000043:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017569,000044:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017570,000045:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017571,000046:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017572,000047:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017573,000048:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017574,000049: 
017575,000050: 
017576,000051:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017577,000052: 
017578,000053:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017579,000054:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017580,000055:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017581,000056:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017582,000057:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017583,000058: 
017584,000059:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017585,000060:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017586,000061:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017587,000062:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017588,000063: 
017589,000064:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017590,000065:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017591,000066:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017592,000067:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017593,000068:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017594,000069: 
017595,000070: 
017596,000071:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
017597,000072: 
017598,000073:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017599,000074:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017600,000075:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 403 

017602,000077:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017603,000078:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017604,000079:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017605,000080:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017606,000081:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017607,000082:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017608,000083:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017609,000084:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017610,000085:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017611,000086:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017612,000087: 
017613,000088:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017614,000089:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017615,000090:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017616,000091: 
017617,000092: 
017618,000093:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017619,000094: 
017620,000095:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017621,000096:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017622,000097:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017623,000098: 
017624,000099:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017625,000100:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017626,000101:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017627,000102:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017628,000103:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017629,000104:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017630,000105:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017631,000106: 
017632,000107:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017633,000108:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017634,000109: 
017635,000110: 
017636,000111:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017637,000112: 
017638,000113:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017639,000114:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017640,000115:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017641,000116:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017642,000117: 
017643,000118: 
017644,000119:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017645,000120: 
017646,000121:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017647,000122:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017648,000123:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017649,000124:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017650,000125: 
017651,000126:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 404 

017653,000128:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017654,000129: 
017655,000130: 
017656,000131:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017657,000132: 
017658,000133:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017659,000134:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017660,000135: 
017661,000136:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017662,000137:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017663,000138:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017664,000139:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017665,000140: 
017666,000141:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017667,000142:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017668,000143: 
017669,000144:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017670,000145:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017671,000146:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017672,000147:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017673,000148: 
017674,000149:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017675,000150:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017676,000151: 
017677,000152:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017678,000153:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017679,000154: 
017680,000155:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017681,000156: 
017682,000157:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017683,000158:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017684,000159:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017685,000160:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017686,000161: 
017687,000162:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017688,000163:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017689,000164: 
017690,000165:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017691,000166:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017692,000167: 
017693,000168: 
017694,000169:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017695,000170:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017696,000171:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://www.ibiblio.org/apollo/hrst/archive/1706.pdf --- MAS 11/2016.)

017702,000177:

017704,000179:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 405 

017706,000181:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
017707,000182: 
017708,000183:                                                                                                  #                       HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
017709,000184: 
017710,000185: 
017711,000186:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
017712,000187: 
017713,000188: 
017714,000189:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017715,000190: 
017716,000191:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017717,000192:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017718,000193:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017719,000194:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017720,000195:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017721,000196:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017722,000197:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017723,000198:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017724,000199:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017725,000200:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017726,000201:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017727,000202:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017728,000203:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017729,000204:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017730,000205:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017731,000206:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017732,000207:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017733,000208:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017734,000209:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017735,000210:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017736,000211:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017737,000212:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017738,000213:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
017739,000214:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017740,000215:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017741,000216:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017742,000217:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017743,000218:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017744,000219:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017745,000220:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017746,000221:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017747,000222:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017748,000223:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017749,000224:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017750,000225:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017751,000226:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017752,000227: 
017753,000228: 
017754,000229:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

Page 406 

017756,000231:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
017757,000232:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
017758,000233:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
017759,000234: 
017760,000235:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
017761,000236:                                                                                                  #  WDRET    =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
017762,000237:                                                                                                  #  DECRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
017763,000238:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG =      INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
017764,000239: 
017765,000240:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET =      POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
017766,000241:                                                                                                  #  CHAR     =      POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
017767,000242:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT    =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
017768,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT  =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
017769,000244: 
017770,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNON    =      VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
017771,000246:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM  =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
017772,000247:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
017773,000248:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
017774,000249: 
017775,000250:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
017776,000251:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017777,000252:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017778,000253:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017779,000254:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
017780,000255:                                                                                                  #  CODE     =      VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
017781,000256:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
017782,000257:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN  =      VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017783,000258:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1.
017784,000259:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP  =      VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
017785,000260:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017786,000261: 
017787,000262:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
017788,000263: 
017789,000264:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET   =      DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
017790,000265: 
017791,000266:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT    =      DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
017792,000267:                                                                                                  #  INREL    =      DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR ( X,Y,Z, REG )
017793,000268: 
017794,000269:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM =      MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
017795,000270:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR    =      MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
017796,000271: 
017797,000272:                                                                                                  #  TEM1     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017798,000273:                                                                                                  #  DSREL    =      TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
017799,000274: 
017800,000275:                                                                                                  #  TEM2     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017801,000276:                                                                                                  #  DSMAG    =      TEM2            MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
017802,000277:                                                                                                  #  IDADDTEM =      TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
017803,000278: 
017804,000279:                                                                                                  #  TEM3     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017805,000280:                                                                                                  #  COUNT    =      TEM3            FOR DSPIN
017806,000281:

017808,000283:                                                                                                  #  TEM4     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
017809,000284:                                                                                                  #  LSTPTR   =      TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
017810,000285:                                                                                                  #  RELRET   =      TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
017811,000286:                                                                                                  #  FREERET  =      TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
017812,000287:                                                                                                  #  DSPWDRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
017813,000288:                                                                                                  #  SEPSCRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
017814,000289:                                                                                                  #  SEPMNRET =      TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN

017818,000293: 
017819,000294:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM  ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
017820,000295:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
017821,000296:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017822,000297:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, - IDAD3TEM-2.
017823,000298:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017824,000299:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, - IDAD3TEM-1.
017825,000300:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
017826,000301:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
017827,000302:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
017828,000303:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017829,000304: 
017830,000305: 
017831,000306:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017832,000307: 
017833,000308:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
017834,000309:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
017835,000310:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
017836,000311:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
017837,000312:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
017838,000313:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
017839,000314: 
017840,000315: 
017841,000316:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
017842,000317:

017844,000319:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK   ERASE                  BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
017845,000320:                                                                                                  #                                                                          RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)

017857,000332:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
017858,000333:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
017859,000334:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
017860,000335:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
017861,000336:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
017862,000337:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
017863,000338:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
017864,000339:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
017865,000340:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
017866,000341:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
017867,000342:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
017868,000343:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

(003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017870,000345: 
017871,000346: 
017872,000347:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017873,000348:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017874,000349:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017875,000350:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017876,000351:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017877,000352:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017878,000353: 
017879,000354:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017880,000355:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017881,000356:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017882,000357:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017883,000358:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017884,000359:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017885,000360: 
017886,000361:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017887,000362:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1    11       ALL ARE OCTAL
017888,000363:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2    10
017889,000364:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3    7
017890,000365:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4    6
017891,000366:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5    5
017892,000367:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1    4
017893,000368:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2    3
017894,000369:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3    2
017895,000370:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4    1
017896,000371:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5    0
017897,000372:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017898,000373: 
017899,000374: 
017900,000375:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017901,000376: 
017902,000377:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017903,000378:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017904,000379:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017905,000380:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017906,000381:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017907,000382:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 409 

017909,000384:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017910,000385:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017911,000386:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017912,000387:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017913,000388:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017914,000389:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017915,000390:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017916,000391:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017917,000392: 
017918,000393: 
017919,000394:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017920,000395:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000

017922,000397:                                                                                                  #  1          00011

017928,000403:                                                                                                  #  7          10011

018651,001126: 41,2401           61447                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
018652,001127:

Page 426 

018654,001129:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018655,001130:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018656,001131:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018657,001132:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018658,001133:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018659,001134:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018660,001135: 
018661,001136:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018662,001137:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018663,001138: 
018664,001139:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018665,001140: 
018666,001141:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018667,001142:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018668,001143:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018669,001144: 
018670,001145:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018671,001146:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018672,001147:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018673,001148:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018674,001149:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018675,001150:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018676,001151: 
018677,001152:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018678,001153:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018679,001154:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018680,001155:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018681,001156:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018682,001157: 
018683,001158:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018684,001159:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018685,001160:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018686,001161:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018687,001162:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018688,001163:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018689,001164:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018690,001165:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018691,001166: 
018692,001167: 
018693,001168:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018694,001169:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018695,001170:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018696,001171: 
018697,001172: 
018698,001173:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018699,001174:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018700,001175: 
018701,001176:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018702,001177:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018703,001178:

Page 427 

018705,001180:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018706,001181: 41,2402           44743        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018707,001182: 41,2403           02453                           TC       COMPTEST

019920,002395:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019921,002396:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019922,002397:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED

019924,002399:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019925,002400: 
019926,002401:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019927,002402:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019928,002403:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019929,002404:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019930,002405:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019931,002406:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019932,002407:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019933,002408: 
019934,002409:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019935,002410:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019936,002411:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019937,002412: 
019938,002413:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019939,002414:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019940,002415: 
019941,002416:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019942,002417:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019943,002418: 
019944,002419:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
019945,002420: 41,3302                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN                              
019946,002421: 
019947,002422: 41,3302                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019948,002423: 41,3302           43311        MONITOR            CS       BIT15/14

020072,002547:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
020073,002548:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
020074,002549:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
020075,002550: 
020076,002551:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
020077,002552: 
020078,002553:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
020079,002554:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
020080,002555:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
020081,002556: 
020082,002557:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
020083,002558:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
020084,002559:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
020085,002560: 
020086,002561: 41,3425           34310        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
020087,002562: 41,3426           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
020088,002563: 41,3427           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
020089,002564: 41,3430           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
020090,002565: 41,3431           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
020091,002566: 41,3432           04642                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

020523,002998:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
020524,002999:

Page 465 

020526,003001:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020527,003002: 
020528,003003:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020529,003004: 
020530,003005:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020531,003006:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020532,003007:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020533,003008:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020534,003009: 
020535,003010:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020536,003011:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020537,003012:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020538,003013: 
020539,003014:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020540,003015:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020541,003016:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020542,003017:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020543,003018:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020544,003019:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020545,003020:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020546,003021:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020547,003022:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020548,003023:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020549,003024:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020550,003025: 
020551,003026: 40,3517           44742        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020552,003027: 40,3520           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020553,003028: 40,3521           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020554,003029: 40,3522           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020555,003030: 40,3523           34727                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020556,003031: 40,3524           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020557,003032: 40,3525           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020558,003033: 40,3526           03535                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020559,003034: 40,3527           04450        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020560,003035: 40,3530           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020561,003036: 40,3531           03533                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020562,003037: 40,3532           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020563,003038: 40,3533           04626                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020564,003039: 40,3534           21062                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020565,003040: 40,3535           34746        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020566,003041: 40,3536           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020567,003042: 40,3537           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020568,003043: 40,3540           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020569,003044: 40,3541           04473                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020570,003045: 40,3542           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020571,003046: 
020572,003047: 40,3543                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020573,003048:

Page 466 

020575,003050:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020576,003051:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020577,003052:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020578,003053:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020579,003054:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020580,003055: 
020581,003056:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020582,003057:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020583,003058:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020584,003059: 
020585,003060:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020586,003061:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020587,003062: 
020588,003063:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020589,003064:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020590,003065:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020591,003066:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020592,003067:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020593,003068: 
020594,003069:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020595,003070:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020596,003071:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020597,003072:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020598,003073: 
020599,003074:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020600,003075:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020601,003076:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020602,003077:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020603,003078:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020604,003079:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020605,003080:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020606,003081: 
020607,003082:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020608,003083:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020609,003084: 
020610,003085:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020611,003086:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020612,003087: 
020613,003088:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020614,003089:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020615,003090: 
020616,003091:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020617,003092:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020618,003093:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020619,003094:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020620,003095:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020621,003096:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020622,003097:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020623,003098: 
020624,003099:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 467 

020626,003101:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020627,003102:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020628,003103:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020629,003104:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020630,003105:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020631,003106:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020632,003107:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020633,003108:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020634,003109:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020635,003110: 
020636,003111:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020637,003112:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020638,003113: 
020639,003114:    4145                                           SETLOC   MID7       +1                         
020640,003115:    4145                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020641,003116:    4145           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS

020744,003219:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS ).
