020747,003222:    4175                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020748,003223:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020749,003224:    4175           34726        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020750,003225:    4176           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020751,003226:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020752,003227:    4177           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020753,003228: 
020754,003229: 
020755,003230:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020756,003231:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020757,003232:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020758,003233:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020759,003234:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020760,003235: 
020761,003236: 
020762,003237:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020763,003238:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020764,003239:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020765,003240:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020766,003241:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020767,003242:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020768,003243:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020769,003244:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020770,003245:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020771,003246:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020772,003247: 
020773,003248: 
020774,003249:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
020775,003250:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020776,003251:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS

Page 470 

020778,003253:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020779,003254:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020780,003255:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020781,003256: 
020782,003257:    4200           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020783,003258:    4201           04211                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020784,003259:    4202           04215                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020785,003260:    4203           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020786,003261:    4204           75003                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020787,003262:    4205           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020788,003263:    4206           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020789,003264:    4207           05124                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020790,003265: 
020791,003266: 
020792,003267:    4210           05146        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020793,003268: 
020794,003269: 
020795,003270:    4211           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020796,003271:    4212           04220                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020837,003312: 
020838,003313: 
020839,003314:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
020840,003315:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
020841,003316:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
020842,003317:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
020843,003318: 
020844,003319:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT IS RESTORED TO STATE IT WAS IN BEFORE BLANKSUB WAS EXECUTED.
020845,003320: 
020846,003321:    4246           74750        BLANKSUB           MASK     SEVEN

020848,003323:    4250           34727                           CAF      BIT14

Page 478 

021133,003608:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021134,003609: 
021135,003610:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021136,003611:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021137,003612:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021138,003613:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021139,003614: 
021140,003615:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021141,003616:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021142,003617:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021143,003618:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021144,003619:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021145,003620:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021146,003621:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021147,003622: 
021148,003623: 
021149,003624:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021150,003625:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021151,003626:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021152,003627:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021153,003628:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021154,003629: 
021155,003630: 
021156,003631:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021157,003632:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021158,003633:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021159,003634:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021160,003635:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021161,003636: 
021162,003637: 
021163,003638:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021164,003639:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021165,003640:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021166,003641: 
021167,003642: 
021168,003643:                                                                                                  #  .
021169,003644: 
021170,003645: 
021171,003646:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021172,003647:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021173,003648:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL
021174,003649:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021175,003650: 
021176,003651: 
021177,003652:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021178,003653:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021179,003654:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021180,003655:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021181,003656:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021182,003657:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 479

021209,003684:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
